Task ID: location-landing-pages-batch
Agent: main
Task: Build ~70 Scottish location landing pages (Glasgow, Edinburgh, Aberdeen, Dundee, etc.) — required a new LocationDetail data type and page template, each showing all 98 services available in that location.

Work Log:
- Reviewed project state: 30 locations listed in site-data.ts (locationCategories nav array) — all with href "#" placeholders. No /locations/ route folder existed. Industry landing pages had been completed in the previous batch (24 industries).
- Designed a new LocationDetail data type in src/lib/location-detail-data.ts with 16 fields per location: slug, name, region, populationNote, tagline, heroHeadline, heroSubhead, heroImage, metaTitle, metaDescription, overviewParagraphs (3 deep paragraphs each), localContext (5-7 Scottish-specific notes), stats (4 KPIs), areas (6-8 neighbourhoods with descriptions), processSteps (4 standardised steps), testimonials (3 client quotes), faqs (6 Q&As), nearbyLocations (up to 6 cross-links), gallery (4 images), servicesByCategory (re-exported shared catalog).
- Created shared services catalog at src/lib/shared-services-catalog.ts with 98 services across 8 categories (Residential 20, Commercial 17, Janitorial 11, Specialty 7, Medical 9, Industrial 2, Outdoor 12, Add-On 23) — all linked to live /services/<slug> routes. This same catalog is reused on every location page (because every Maundy Clean service is available in every Scottish location).
- Built 10 reusable location-detail section components in src/components/location-detail/: location-hero, location-overview, location-stats, location-areas, location-services, location-process, location-testimonials, location-gallery, location-faq, location-nearby, location-final-cta. Each component is client-side with Framer Motion animations, brand tokens (var(--brand), var(--gold), var(--cream)), responsive grids, and accessibility-conscious markup. The location-services component renders the full 98-service catalog grouped by 8 categories.
- Wrote a single consolidated Python generator script (scripts/generate_location_exports.py) that defines all 72 Scottish locations grouped into 6 regions (Greater Glasgow 12, Edinburgh & Lothians 10, Fife & Central 12, Aberdeen & Grampian 10, Highlands & Islands 14, Borders & South-West 14). Each location has bespoke neighbourhoods and local context notes — Glasgow covers West End/Merchant City/South Side etc., Edinburgh covers New Town/Old Town/Marchmont/Leith etc., Highlands locations include island ferry-port context (Kirkwall/Lerwick/Stornoway/Portree). The script uses 7 reusable template generators (overviewParagraphs, stats, processSteps, testimonials, faqs, nearby, gallery) that personalise around the location name and region. Generated 72 location exports appended to location-detail-data.ts — file is now 5,622 lines / 745 KB.
- Created 72 page.tsx files under src/app/locations/<slug>/ via scripts/create_location_pages.py. Each page follows the 11-section render pattern: LocationHero → LocationOverview → LocationStats → LocationAreas → LocationServices → LocationProcess → LocationTestimonials → LocationGallery → LocationFaq → LocationNearby → LocationFinalCta — wrapped in SiteHeader / SiteFooter / MobileStickyCta.
- Generated updated locationCategories block via scripts/gen_site_data_locations.py (72 locations, 6 regions, all with live /locations/<slug> hrefs). Task ID: global-floating-buttons-and-ai-chatbot
Agent: main (continuation)
Task: Design a fixed WhatsApp icon/button as global (every page) alongside a chatbot icon globally that links with an AI RAG chatbot.

Work Log:
- Invoked LLM skill to learn z-ai-web-dev-sdk chat completions API pattern (backend-only, system prompt via 'assistant' role, thinking: disabled for standard responses).
- Inspected project: Next.js 16, z-ai-web-dev-sdk v0.0.18 installed, framer-motion v12.23.2 available, contactInfo.phone = "+44 7735 322362", brand tokens --brand/--brand-dark/--brand-light/--gold/--gold-dark, MobileStickyCta already exists but only on mobile + only after scroll.
- Created /home/z/my-project/src/lib/chat-knowledge-base.ts:
  - RAG_KNOWLEDGE_BASE constant with full company context: services list, pricing tiers, locations served, trust/safety facts, common FAQ answers, internal links, assistant behaviour rules.
  - CHATBOT_SYSTEM_PROMPT constant wraps the knowledge base with role/behaviour instructions.
- Created /home/z/my-project/src/app/api/chat/route.ts (POST endpoint):
  - Runtime: nodejs (z-ai-web-dev-sdk not Edge-compatible).
  - Accepts { message, sessionId, history } JSON body.
  - Merges client-side history with server-side conversation store (in-memory Map, MAX_MESSAGES=12 to prevent token overflow).
  - Calls zai.chat.completions.create({ messages, thinking: { type: 'disabled' } }).
  - Returns { success, response, sessionId, timestamp }.
  - Graceful fallback: on any error, returns 200 with a "please call" message so the chat UI doesn't crash.
  - GET endpoint for health checks.
- Created /home/z/my-project/src/components/floating-buttons.tsx ("use client"):
  - Fixed bottom-right floating buttons: WhatsApp (#25D366 green, branded SVG) + Chatbot (brand gradient with Sparkles icon).
  - WhatsApp deep link: wa.me/447735322362 with prefilled "Hello Maundy Clean..." message.
  - Pulse rings + hover tooltips on both buttons.
  - Chat panel: opens/closes with animation, header (avatar + online status), scrollable messages area, input bar with send button, footer with phone number.
  - Quick-reply chips: "How much is a recurring clean?", "Do you cover Edinburgh?", etc. — shown only when chat is fresh.
  - Loading state: animated 3-dot typing indicator.
  - New-message badge: shows on chatbot button when AI replies and chat is closed.
  - Conversation history: last 8 messages sent to API for multi-turn context; sessionStorage for sessionId persistence.
  - FormattedBotText: linkifies internal paths (/services/x, /quote, /locations) and external URLs in AI responses.
  - Reset button (RotateCcw icon) to clear chat.
- Updated /home/z/my-project/src/app/layout.tsx to import FloatingButtons and render it after <Toaster />, making it global on every page.
- Ran TypeScript check (npx tsc --noEmit --skipLibCheck): zero errors in src/.
- Verified HTTP 200 on / (home), /api/chat (GET health), and /services/spring-cleaning (sample service page).
- Verified FloatingButtons render on home page and service page (grep for wa.me/447735322362, "Maundy AI Assistant", "Ask Maundy AI").
- Tested /api/chat with 2 sample queries:
  - "Hi, how much is a recurring clean?" → AI correctly quoted £62/visit, mentioned PVG-checked + 30-day re-clean guarantee, linked to /quote + phone (all facts from RAG knowledge base).
  - "Do you cover Edinburgh for spring cleaning?" → AI correctly confirmed Edinburgh coverage, mentioned 64-point checklist, photo report, £22/hr, linked to /quote + phone.

Stage Summary:
- WhatsApp floating button: green branded SVG, fixed bottom-right, links to wa.me/447735322362 with prefilled enquiry message. Global on every page.
- AI RAG chatbot: floating Sparkles button next to WhatsApp, opens a 600px chat panel with online status, quick-reply chips, animated typing indicator, linkified AI responses, and reset button.

Amenity &amp; Facility Hygiene", "Site Survey &amp; Bespoke Plan", "Fabric &amp; Upholstery Restoration") were being rendered by React as text content — React HTML-escapes the `&` to `&amp;`, producing `&amp;amp;` in the HTML output (double-encoded), which displays as the literal text "&amp;" to the user. Fixed by changing all 6 title strings to use literal `&` instead of `&amp;` (React will then correctly escape `&` → `&amp;` → displays as `&` to user). Post-fix verification confirmed the HTML now contains `&amp;` (single-encoded) which displays as `&` to the user. Note: this same bug exists in salon-spa-cleaning-seo.tsx titles like "Specialised Sanitisation &amp; Fogging" — salon-spa precedent was not followed here because the brief explicitly directs these titles to use literal `&` and the visible "&amp;" text on screen would be a clear visual bug. The fix is contained to auto-dealership only — salon-spa was not modified.
- Discovered during verification that the dev server (Next.js 16.1.3 Turbopack on port 3000) had stopped accepting connections between shell sessions (background processes were being killed when the parent Bash shell exited). Worked around this by starting the dev server with `npm run dev > /tmp/dev_run.log 2>&1 &` and running all curl-based verification checks within the SAME Bash call (using the Bash tool's timeout=90000ms), then killing the dev server at the end of the call. All 7 verification checks pass.
